  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_32bd9b4d-1d72-4e79-91c0-bcfa11bb8652'
      });

<span id="freeTextContainer5484406989881161910">Not Business as Usual<br/><br/>In the current business climate of distrust, cynicism, and fear, Scott Weiss offers a radical challenge to those of us who lead others.  His call for authentic leadership means dropping the mask of the Executive Persona as well as the camouflage and doubletalk of traditional corporate communications.  It demands an end to our self-deceptions and the de</span>
  <span id="freeText5484406989881161910" style="display:none">Not Business as Usual<br /><br />In the current business climate of distrust, cynicism, and fear, Scott Weiss offers a radical challenge to those of us who lead others.  His call for authentic leadership means dropping the mask of the Executive Persona as well as the camouflage and doubletalk of traditional corporate communications.  It demands an end to our self-deceptions and the deception of others in the name of business as usual. Those who are brave enough to accept his DARE will discover...<br />•    More loyal, satisfied clients and customers<br />•    Reduced turnover and more<br />•    engaged employees<br />•    A more creative, innovative, and collaborative workplace<br />•    Less personal conflict and more genuine relationships<br />•    The passion to thrive, not just survive, in our professions<br /><br />A courageous book that calls on leaders themselves to step up and make the changes that will rebuild trust and restore business integrity for customers, employees, and the global public.<br /><br /><br /></span>

    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2548038011?book_show_action=true">Oct 01, 2018</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="CGY Reviews" class="user" itemprop="url" name="CGY Reviews" href="/user/show/80007601-cgy-reviews">CGY Reviews</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2548038011" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13109580549392797215">Dare: Accepting the Challenge of Trusting Leadership by Scott Weiss challenges the status quo that is current in business today. Weiss asserts that leaders in business must change the way they do things in order to fully impact business for the better. While not a strict how to book, Weiss lays out strategies and a way of thinking that can radically change how business is done, how relationships are forged in the workplace, and how trust has a way of working to one's benefit. All of this in turn</span>
  <span id="freeText13109580549392797215" style="display:none">Dare: Accepting the Challenge of Trusting Leadership by Scott Weiss challenges the status quo that is current in business today. Weiss asserts that leaders in business must change the way they do things in order to fully impact business for the better. While not a strict how to book, Weiss lays out strategies and a way of thinking that can radically change how business is done, how relationships are forged in the workplace, and how trust has a way of working to one's benefit. All of this in turn will lead to more customers, and more satisfied customers, reduced employee turnover, and happier employees, along with a more creative and adaptive workplace. Lofty goals indeed, but Weiss makes these notions seem doable. Overall, the key to success in business is communication, which starts at the top, and works its way down. How effective and clear this communication is matters most in every day business. Highly recommend this engaging and worthwhile business strategy book.<br /><br /></span>

          </span>

<span id="freeTextContainer16607681866433818017">Dare: Accepting the Challenge of Trusting Leadership by Scott Weiss challenges the status quo that is current in business today. Weiss asserts that leaders in business must change the way they do things in order to fully impact business for the better. While not a strict how to book, Weiss lays out strategies and a way of thinking that can radically change how business is done, how relationships are forged in the workplace, and how trust has a way of working to one's benefit.   <span id="freeText16607681866433818017" style="display:none">Dare: Accepting the Challenge of Trusting Leadership by Scott Weiss challenges the status quo that is current in business today. Weiss asserts that leaders in business must change the way they do things in order to fully impact business for the better. While not a strict how to book, Weiss lays out strategies and a way of thinking that can radically change how business is done, how relationships are forged in the workplace, and how trust has a way of working to one's benefit. All of this in turn will lead to more customers, and more satisfied customers, reduced employee turnover, and happier employees, along with a more creative and adaptive workplace. Lofty goals indeed, but Weiss makes these notions seem doable. Overall, the key to success in business is communication, which starts at the top, and works its way down. How effective and clear this communication is matters most in every day business. Highly recommend this engaging and worthwhile business strategy book. </span>

<div id="review_2543970487" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2543970487" />
    <a title="Lust for Lit" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/74624063-lust-for-lit"><img alt="Lust for Lit" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1512485063p2/74624063.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2543970487?book_show_action=true">Sep 27, 2018</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Lust for Lit" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Lust for Lit" href="/user/show/74624063-lust-for-lit">Lust for Lit</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2543970487" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16127256502297998579">'Dare' by Scott Weiss will serve as a useful book for any business leaders who are unsure of how to lead their staff in a society where distrusting those with authority is the norm. Weiss stresses that this distrust can have a massive impact on businesses if it is not addressed directly and quickly. He advocates transparency from leaders to dispel the distrust that so many workers feel towards their employers. Honesty is key in today's society and Weiss shows how true this is with real-life exam</span>
  <span id="freeText16127256502297998579" style="display:none">'Dare' by Scott Weiss will serve as a useful book for any business leaders who are unsure of how to lead their staff in a society where distrusting those with authority is the norm. Weiss stresses that this distrust can have a massive impact on businesses if it is not addressed directly and quickly. He advocates transparency from leaders to dispel the distrust that so many workers feel towards their employers. Honesty is key in today's society and Weiss shows how true this is with real-life examples of business leaders who have adopted a transparent management strategy and the benefits of doing so. 'Dare' shows that a more ethical and honest approach to business leadership can make an operation run so more smoothly and efficiently. Perhaps the idea is simple, but in a world where there is so much dishonesty and distrust, it could be revolutionary.</span>
  <a data-text-id="16127256502297998579" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_456212299" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/456212299" />
    <a title="P.K." class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/1149545-p-k"><img alt="P.K." src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1372361016p2/1149545.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/456212299?book_show_action=true">Nov 14, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="P.K." class="user" itemprop="url" name="P.K." href="/user/show/1149545-p-k">P.K.</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer456212299" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2323249490080806344">As a whole, we have become increasingly distrustful of the voices projected by our leaders and others in positions of authority. This did not occur by accident or misunderstanding. It was a gradual yet steady erosion caused by deceits revealed after that fact. Some of these deceits were large scale, causing financial ruin for thousands. Others are grayer, small deceptions that, however well intended, are instead communicating a message of untrustworthiness. But, as Scott Weiss explains in his bo</span>
  <span id="freeText2323249490080806344" style="display:none">As a whole, we have become increasingly distrustful of the voices projected by our leaders and others in positions of authority. This did not occur by accident or misunderstanding. It was a gradual yet steady erosion caused by deceits revealed after that fact. Some of these deceits were large scale, causing financial ruin for thousands. Others are grayer, small deceptions that, however well intended, are instead communicating a message of untrustworthiness. But, as Scott Weiss explains in his book DARE: Accepting the Challenge of Trusting Leadership, this doesn’t have to be the status quo. “My concern is for each person to find a way of leading that is congruent with who they really are. To do this we first need to know our own core values and beliefs, be able to communicate them to others, and then ensure that our actions always match our words.”<br /><br />His passion for authentic and trustworthy communication began when he confronted, voluntarily no less, his own executive persona viewed on video during a leadership development program. Glaringly obvious to him, and the other industry leaders in the program, was that his projected persona was not a like-able individual, much less trustworthy. More disheartening to him, was that this image conflicted with who he felt was his authentic self. That rift, he decided, had to change. Thus began his quest and passion to align his values, behavior and word across the board.<br /><br />In DARE, Weiss provides numerous real world examples of leaders who also took up the challenge to be as good as their word. This book will inspire you to take action and move the default position back to trust. For leaders and society as a whole, it is not only possible, it is necessary.</span>
  <a data-text-id="2323249490080806344" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_2472012046" class="review notext nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2472012046" />
    <a title="Graham Davies" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/74430272-graham-davies"><img alt="Graham Davies" src="https://s.gr-assets.com/assets/nophoto/user/m_50x66-82093808bca726cb3249a493fbd3bd0f.png" /></a>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('/p21zj6EH6wBtsYBq192y81Le2z+qcPk2LCEoJ/uUtVq+maxA+qfHMoV1iBQ3DSNQ5QHF1oXrM2JYTK64d7DBg==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {

  }
